 Praising some states in bringing the food grains received from the Center to the poor people under the Public Distribution System, Pawar said that the Central Government gave the farmers a fair price for their crops, but the price of the grains received by the poor Did not increase bhartiya dalhan anusandhan santhaan (aiipiar) main shanivaar ko hone vaale ek kaarykram main bhaag lene aaye krishi mantri ne patrakaron se baatcheet main mahangaai par puche gayi sawaalon ko najar andaaj karte huye kaha ki kendra sarkaar kaa kaam krishi kaa acha utpaadan karnaa, kisaanon se use uchit mulya par khareednaa or phir use godaamon tak pahunchaana he

 yahi haal kuch saal 2017 main hue vidhansabha chunaav main bhi rahaa he

 Let's know some special things about him on his birthday: 1
 nitu kapur kaa janm 8 july 1958 ko dilli main hua tha
 2
 khabaron ke mutabik nitu singh kaa asli naam 'sonia singh' tha lekin filmon main aane ke baad inkaa naam 'nitu singh' ho gaya or abhinayta rishi kapur ke saath shaadi ke baad 'nitu kapur' ban gayi
 Neetu Singh's real name is also called 'harmeet Kaur' in some places
 3
 Neetu Singh started acting as a child, in the 60s, he did films like 'do Kaliyan', 'pious Papi' and 'waris' as child artists and in those days his screen name was 'baby Neetu' or There used to be 'baby Sonia'
 4
 Neetu was a child actress from Vyjantimala's dance school in her childhood, and from there Vyjantimala asked Neetu to work as a child artist in the film 'sooraj'
 5
 Neetu Kapoor's mother 'raji Singh' also played the role of Neetu's mother on screen in the film 'rani Aur Lalpari'
 6
 Neetu Kapoor was married to Rishi Kapoor on 13 April 1979 and then she quit acting

 7
 nitu singh ne abhinayta jithendra kii film 'vaaris' main child artist kaa kirdaar nibhaayaa tha or kai saalon ke baad 70 ke dashak main jithendra ke saath hi 'priytama' main lead role kiya tha
 8
 khabaron ke mutabik 1975 main nitu kapur sabase vyast adaakara maani jaati thi or lagbhag 85 filmein unke haath main thi or unamem se adhiktar rishi kapur, randhir kapur or shashi kapur ke saath thi
 9
 film 'besharm' main nitu kapur ne bete ranbir kapur ke saath pehali baar kaam kiya tha
 10

 Understand what changes have been made in the new bill
 
 
 1
 What will happen on bail? According to the ordinance, now it will not be so easy for the husband to get bail
 jab magistrate patni kaa paksh nahin sun letaa tab tak shuhar ko zamaanat nahin milegi
 2
 kya ho paaegaa samjhauta?ab donon pakshon ke bich samjhauta patni kii pahal par hi ho saktaa he
 That is, once the matter reaches the court, there will be a court agreement
 agar maamla saamne aane ke baad shuhar sulah karnaa chahta he, to patni kaa bhi maananaa zaruri hoga
 3
 naaballig bachche kaa kya hoga?agar talaak ke samay pati-patni kaa koi naaballig baccha he, tab tak bachche maa ke paas hi rahenge
 And on the court's order, the husband will have to pay alimony to the woman and child
 4
 What will happen to the compensation? If the husband appeals for bail, he will get bail only when he asks for compensation to the wife
 or muaavze kii raashi kitni hogi, iskaa faisla magistrate hi karenge
 5
 kya puraane cese par lagu hoga kanoon?agar shuhar par koi isi tarah kaa maamla pehle se chal rahaa he, to ye nae praavdhaan usapar lagu nahin honge
 If a case comes up where the crime is going on continuously, then the court can decide on its own
 6
 Are the major amendments made? - Magistrate can give bail to the accused by hearing the victim's side before the trial
 - peedita, parijan or khun ke rishtedaar hi exiaar darj kara sakate hai
 - The magistrate shall have the right to maintain the marriage by making an agreement between the husband and wife
